***catfish.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a> (94695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cat</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fish</i>. Likely so named for its prominent barbels like a cat's <a href = vnd.unilang:whiskers.html>whiskers</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">catfishes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>any fish of the order Siluriformes, mainly found in fresh water, lacking scales, and having barbels like <a href = vnd.unilang:whiskers.html>whiskers</a> around the mouth
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">catlet</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Africa</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sheat</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sheatfish</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">catfishes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">catfishing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">catfished</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To fish for <a class="mw-selflink selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></a>
<dl><dd><i>I only use this rod for <b>catfishing</b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the 2010 documentary <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catfish_(film)" class="extiw" title="w:Catfish (film)"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>Catfish</a></a></i>, supposedly inspired by the practice of fishermen <a href = vnd.unilang:keeping.html>keeping</a> cod active by <a href = vnd.unilang:storing.html>storing</a> them with <a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a> (see sense 1) which nip at their <a href = vnd.unilang:tails.html>tails</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">catfishes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone who creates a fake profile on a social media platform in order to deceive people.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Such a fake profile.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">catfishes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">catfishing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">catfished</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Internet<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To create and operate a fake online profile to deceive (someone).
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> January 17,  <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Pilon,  “In <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a>’<a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a> Story, Deception Ripped From the Screen”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_New_York_Times" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The New York Times">The New York Times</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2013/01/18/sports/ncaafootball/deception-ripped-from-the-screen-in-hoax-story-of-manti-teo.html">[1]</a></sup>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Serial_Number" class="extiw" title="w:International Standard Serial Number">ISSN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/issn/0362-4331">0362-4331</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Getting <b>catfished</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> when someone falls for a person online who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not necessarily real. It can involve pictures, phone calls, social media profiles, text messages, e-mails and <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> phony friends or family members.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> January 16,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Donald_Glover" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Donald Glover">Donald <a href = vnd.unilang:glover.html>Glover</a></a> as <a href = vnd.unilang:troy.html>Troy</a>,  <cite>Cooperative Polygraphy</cite> ('<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Community_(TV_series)" class="extiw" title="w:Community (TV series)">Community</a>'), season 5, episode 4, NBC, 12:17 from the start:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><i>[to Abed]</i> You made a profile for a fake dude and lured her into an online relationship. <i>[to Annie]</i> He's <b>catfishing</b> you.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><span class="see-cites">For more quotations using this term, see Citations:<a href = vnd.unilang:catfish.html>catfish</a>.</span></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***catwalk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:catwalk.html>catwalk</a> (34334)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cat</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">walk</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catwalk.html>catwalk</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:catwalks.html>catwalks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An elevated enclosed passage providing access fore and aft from the bridge of a merchant vessel.</li>
<li>Any similar elevated walkway.</li>
<li>A narrow elevated stage on which <a href = vnd.unilang:models.html>models</a> parade; a runway</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> "the <a href = vnd.unilang:catwalk.html>catwalk</a>"</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The business of making <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a> for fashion <a href = vnd.unilang:shows.html>shows</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">platform for fashion <a href = vnd.unilang:shows.html>shows</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>: runway</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:catwalk.html>catwalk</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***caviar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:caviar.html>caviar</a> (84395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:caviar.html>caviar</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">caviaro</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">خاویار</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">havyar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">havyar</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خاویار</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xâvyâr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خایه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xâye</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">egg</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">egg</i>). Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ajvar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:caviar.html>caviar</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">caviars</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Roe of the sturgeon or other large fish, considered a delicacy.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something whose flavour <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> too fine for the vulgar taste.</li></ol>
</body> 
***cavil.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a> (37322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">caviller</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mock, jest, rail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cavillor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jeer, mock, satirise, reason captiously</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cavilla</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jeering, raillery, scoffing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">cavillare</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">cavillar</i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">cavilar</i>; nominal usage developed within English from the original verbal usage.<sup id="cite_ref-OED_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-OED-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">cavils</b>, <i>present participle</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cavilling</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">caviling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">cavilled</b> <i>or</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">caviled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To criticise for petty or frivolous reasons.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">be hypercritical</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">nitpick</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">pettifog</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">split hairs</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1598?</b>, William Shakespeare, <i>Two <a href = vnd.unilang:gentlemen.html>Gentlemen</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:verona.html>Verona</a></i>, Act I, scene I:
<dl><dd>'<a href = vnd.unilang:tis.html>Tis</a> love you <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></b> at: I am not Love.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Barr_(writer)" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Barr (writer)">Robert Barr</a>,  chapter 5, in  <cite>Lord Stranleigh Abroad</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL1796924W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Stranleigh found no difficulty in getting a cavalcade together at Bleacher’s station, an amazingly long distance west of New York. A <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> finds little trouble in obtaining what he wants, if he never <b>cavils</b> at the price asked, and <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> willing to pay in advance.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1928</b>,  D. H. Lawrence,  <cite>Lady Chatterley's Lover</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I wish you wouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hilda.html>Hilda</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1976</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_Dawkins" class="extiw" title="w:Richard Dawkins">Richard Dawkins</a>,  <cite>The Selfish Gene</cite>, Kindle edition, OUP Oxford, published 2016, page 368:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But their first supporting quotation, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <i>The Selfish Gene</i>, includes selfish genes that do have phenotypic <a href = vnd.unilang:effects.html>effects</a>. Far it be from <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, however, to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></b> at the honour of being quoted in the <i>Oxford English Dictionary</i>!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">cavils</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A petty or trivial objection or criticism.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1835</b>,  Charles G. Finney,  <cite>Lectures on revivals of religion</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not worth while to spend your time in arguing against a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:cavil.html>cavil</a></b>, but make him feel he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> committing a sin to plead it, and thus enlist his conscience on your side.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ceder.html>ceder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ceder.html>ceder</a></i>, either indirectly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cedre</i> or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cedrus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κέδρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kédros</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of unknown origin.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cel.html>cel</a> (1367)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">celle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cella</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cel.html>cel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cellen.html>cellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:celletje.html>celletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cell <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a compartment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ol><li>component of a battery</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> component of a body tissue</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a small room, such as a prison or cloister cell</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">entomology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cell  |  of a honeycomb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computer science</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cell  |  of a table</li></ol></li></ol>

***celibaat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:celibaat.html>celibaat</a> (25419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">célibat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caelibātus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">celibacy, a single life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caelibare</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">caelebs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unmarried</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***cello.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:cello.html>cello</a> (16873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Shortening of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">violoncello</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">violoncello</i>. Influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:cello.html>Cello</a></i>.
</p>

***celluloid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a> (57893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Former trademark of <a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>Celluloid</a> Manufacturing Company
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/celluloid" class="extiw" title="w:celluloid"><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/celluloid" class="extiw" title="w:celluloid">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">celluloids</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of a variety of thermoplastics created from nitrocellulose and camphor, once used as photographic <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>.
<ul><li><b>1894</b> June, Antonia Dickson, W. K. L. Dickson, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Century_Magazine/Volume_48/Issue_2/Edison%27s_Invention_of_the_Kineto-Phonograph:_Account_of_the_Invention" class="extiw" title="s:Century Magazine/Volume 48/Issue 2/Edison | s Invention of the Kineto-Phonograph: Account of the Invention">Edison's Invention of the Kineto-Phonograph: Account of the Invention</a></i>, article in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Century_Magazine" class="extiw" title="w:Century Magazine">Century Magazine</a></i>, Volume 48, Issue 2,
<dl><dd>Then followed some experiments with <a href = vnd.unilang:drums.html>drums</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> which sheets of sensitized <b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> drawn, the edges being pressed into a narrow <a href = vnd.unilang:slot.html>slot</a> in the surface, similar in construction to the old tin-foil phonograph.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1910</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stephen_Leacock" class="extiw" title="w:Stephen Leacock">Stephen Leacock</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Conjurer%27s_Revenge" class="extiw" title="s:The Conjurer | s Revenge">The Conjurer's Revenge</a></i>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Literary_Lapses" class="extiw" title="s:Literary Lapses">Literary Lapses</a></i>,
<dl><dd>"And will you now, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a>, take off your <b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> collar and permit <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to burn it in the candle? Thank you, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a>. And will you allow <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to smash your spectacles for you with my hammer? Thank you."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> often used attributively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The genre of cinema; <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>.
<ul><li><b>2001</b> August 14, Riki Wilchins, <i>Gender on <b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b></i>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Advocate" class="extiw" title="w:The Advocate">The Advocate</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=B2MEAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA26amp;dq=%22celluloid%22+-intitle:%22celluloid%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=ezPWTc-fEYb-vQPy1rGkBwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=3amp;ved=0CD0Q6AEwAgv=onepageamp;q=%22celluloid%22%20-intitle%3A%22celluloid%22amp;f=false">page 26</a>.</li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b>,  Preston Whaley,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:blows.html>Blows</a> Like a Horn</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=eZefines2DcCamp;pg=PA82amp;dq=%22celluloid%22+-intitle:%22celluloid%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=ezPWTc-fEYb-vQPy1rGkBwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;resnum=37amp;ved=0CO0BEOgBMCQv=onepageamp;q=%22celluloid%22%20-intitle%3A%22celluloid%22amp;f=false">[1]</a></sup>, page 20:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In particular, they set Kerouac and Ginsberg to the specifications of an emergent superficial form—<b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> antiheroes—attractive to those in want of adventure and who would soon be reading <i>On the Road</i> (1957).</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:stof.html>stof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestaande.html>bestaande</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> nitrocellulose <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>.a. <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruikt.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drager.html>drager</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fotografisch.html>fotografische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> cinematografische <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>.</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a>, in contrast <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> video
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:celluloid.html>celluloid</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedraaid.html>gedraaid</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***celmaat.html

***centerfold.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:centerfold.html>centerfold</a> (45720)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">center</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fold</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:centerfold.html>centerfold</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:centerfolds.html>centerfolds</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_and_British_English_spelling_differences" class="extiw" title="w:American and British English spelling differences">American spelling</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>The single sheet of paper that forms the middle two pages of a magazine or other publication.</li>
<li>A large photograph printed on this sheet, typically in the form of a nude, or provocatively dressed, sexually attractive woman or <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</li>
<li>The person appearing in such a photograph.
<ul><li><b>1981</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_J._Geils_Band" class="extiw" title="w:The J. Geils Band">The J. <a href = vnd.unilang:geil.html>Geils</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>Band</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Centerfold_(song)" class="extiw" title="w:Centerfold (song)"><a href = vnd.unilang:centerfold.html>Centerfold</a></a>
<dl><dd><i>My blood <a href = vnd.unilang:runs.html>runs</a> cold / My memory <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> just <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> / My angel <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:centerfold.html>centerfold</a></b></i></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Any very sexually attractive person, who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> therefore material for such a photograph.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">single sheet of paper that forms the middle two pages of a magazine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>:</li>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">centuriō, centuriōnis</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">centum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a hundred</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***ceremonieel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ceremonieel.html>ceremonieel</a> (47651)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cérémoniel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ceremonieel.html>ceremonieel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ceremonieel.html>ceremoniëler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ceremonieelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ceremonial</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
